Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents rely on long-term memory to support extended interactions and personalized assistance beyond finite context windows. Existing memory agents actively update external memory through generated write, revise, and delete operations, but these updates may omit important information, corrupt existing memory, or introduce unsupported hallucinated content. Once stored, such errors become persistent system-state failures that can affect future reasoning and generation. In this paper, we propose TrustMem, a framework designed to improve the trustworthiness of memory consolidation. TrustMem relies on a Memory Transition Verifier to evaluate the transition process of memory updates in terms of coverage, preservation, and faithfulness. It further constructs preference pairs among candidate updates under the same memory state, enabling preference-guided reinforcement learning to directly optimize memory updating behaviors. Extensive experiments demonstrate that TrustMem improves both memory utility and reliability: it achieves state-of-the-art results across MemoryAgentBench, HaluMem, and the Mem-alpha validation set, improves HaluMem memory extraction by 12.14 F1 points, and reduces transition-level omission, corruption, and hallucination by 40.1\%, 79.1\%, and 50.0\%, respectively, compared with the strongest baseline for each error type.

### [157] [Elo-Disentangled Player-Style Embeddings for Human Chess via Rating-Conditioned Residual Move Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25176)
*Jason Carlson*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种残差式个体棋风表征学习框架：通过评分条件基模型（Maia-3+Stockfish特征）捕捉典型走法，再用冻结的基模型锚定一个学习到的走法编码器和每玩家向量z，使z仅解释偏离评分典型走法的偏差。z在Elo正交轴上捕捉风格，线性探针仅能恢复R²=0.06的评分信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有棋风建模难以分离棋力与风格，作者希望学习与Elo近似解耦的、可解释的个体风格表征。

Method: 残差式设计：(1) 评分条件基模型（Maia-3策略logits+Stockfish特征，在Maia-2提议候选上评分）预测典型走法；(2) 冻结基模型锚定走法编码器和每玩家向量z，z仅学习偏差部分；(3) 在22,620个保留决策上评估。

Result: 基模型比Maia-3 NLL降低27-37%（2800+最高）；top-1匹配从Maia-2的0.51到Maia-3的0.57再到引擎增强基模型的0.68；z对原始走法匹配贡献微小，但能跨局识别玩家、线性探针仅恢复R²=0.06的评分。

Conclusion: 强评分条件基模型+紧凑的、与Elo解耦的嵌入是一种经济、可解释的个体风格建模方式，可作为逐玩家偏好微调的替代方案。

Abstract: We study representation learning for individual human chess style: a per-player embedding learned from a player's move history such that inner products measure stylistic similarity, while being approximately disentangled from playing strength (Elo). Our key design is a residual formulation: a rating-conditioned base move model (Maia-3 policy logits plus Stockfish-derived features, scored over Maia-2-proposed candidates) captures what a typical player of a given strength would play, and a frozen copy of it anchors a learned move encoder and a per-player vector z, so that z explains only deviations from rating-typical play. The base model improves move prediction over the strong Maia-3 policy by 27-37% relative NLL across the rating spectrum, with the largest gains at the top (2800+); Stockfish's marginal value grows monotonically with Elo (negligible at 900-1200, +0.085 nats at 2800+). On a shared Elo-stratified benchmark of 22,620 held-out decisions, top-1 move-matching rises monotonically from Maia-2 to Maia-3 to the Stockfish-augmented base (0.51 -> 0.57 -> 0.68): the base is +33% relative top-1 over Maia-2 and +19% over Maia-3 (30% lower NLL), with the engine-feature lift largest at high Elo. The player embedding adds little to raw move-matching on top of this base -- its marginal top-1 gain falls within the 95% confidence interval -- and its value is instead representational: z generalizes to held-out decisions without overfitting, re-identifies players from disjoint games above chance, and a linear probe recovers rating from z with only R^2 = 0.06 (no better nonlinearly), evidence it captures style on an Elo-orthogonal axis. We argue that a strong rating-conditioned base plus a compact, Elo-disentangled embedding -- separating typical play from individual deviation -- is an economical, interpretable model of individual style, an alternative to per-player preference fine-tuning.

### [158] [Transferability for General Reasoning: An Automated Curriculum for Multi-Domain RLVR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25178)
*Yongjin Yang,Jiarui Liu,Yinghui He,Lezhen Zhang,Bernhard Schölkopf,Zhijing Jin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Transfer-Aware Curriculum (TAC)，一种在强化学习与可验证奖励的多领域训练中，通过感知领域间迁移性来自适应调整训练课程的方法，在六个推理领域上取得了最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR训练中，各领域的采样课程（训练频率）通常是固定或手动设定的，但推理技能在不同领域间的迁移是不均匀的。现有的基于可学习性的课程方法只关注当前哪个领域在提升，却忽略了该领域的梯度更新是否能惠及其他领域。

Method: TAC采用bandit风格的在线课程学习，包含两个核心信号：(1) 每个领域的优势函数（advantage）以衡量局部可学习性；(2) 用GRPO步骤中的投影梯度（projected gradients）通过梯度几何对齐（gradient-geometry alignment）来估计跨领域迁移性。该方法几乎零开销（<1% wall-clock overhead）。

Result: 在包含六个领域的推理套件上，分别使用Qwen3-1.7B和Llama3.2-3B进行测试，TAC在宏平均准确率上均优于比例随机采样、手工设计的课程以及仅基于可学习性的bandit方法，相比后者最高提升2.8个点（相对提升10%）。

Conclusion: 跨领域迁移性是RLVR多领域课程设计的关键信号；去除迁移性项后性能显著下降；TAC在不平衡训练混合下保持鲁棒，而仅基于可学习性的课程会过度偏向主导领域。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has been extended from single-domain training to multi-domain reasoning suites spanning mathematics, programming, and science. However, the training curriculum (how often each domain is sampled) is typically fixed or hand-tuned, even though reasoning skills transfer unevenly across domains. Existing learnability-based curricula adapt to where the policy is currently improving, but are blind to whether a gradient step on the selected domain benefits the remaining domains. In this paper, we propose Transfer-Aware Curriculum (TAC), a bandit-style online curriculum that prioritizes domains whose updates broadly benefit the rest of the training suite. TAC repurposes signals already produced by RL training: per-domain advantages capture local learnability, and projected gradients, taken from the GRPO step being computed, estimate cross-domain transferability via gradient-geometry alignment, at negligible cost (<1% wall-clock overhead). Across a six-domain reasoning suite, TAC achieves the best macro-averaged accuracy on both Qwen3-1.7B and Llama3.2-3B, outperforming proportional random sampling, a hand-designed schedule, and a learnability-only bandit, and improving over the last of these by up to 2.8 points (10% relative). Ablations show performance degrades sharply when the transferability term is removed, and TAC remains robust on imbalanced training mixtures where learnability-only curricula over-commit to dominant domains. Our findings establish cross-domain transferability as a key signal for curriculum design in multi-domain RLVR.

### [159] [To Isolate or to Score? Model-Adaptive Assessment for Cost-Efficient Multi-Agent RAG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25191)
*Jungseob Lee,Chanjun Park,Heuiseok Lim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了检索增强生成中多智能体文档评估的关键机制：对于弱基线模型，主要收益来自分离文档以消除上下文混淆（而非评分质量），而强基线模型则依赖评分质量。作者提出MADARA架构，通过诊断阈值实现零样本跨模型泛化，显著降低计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 文档上下文混淆是弱基线模型性能提升的核心瓶颈，而非评估质量本身；MADARA提供了一种鲁棒、轻量级的流水线来消除计算开销，且具有良好的跨模型泛化能力。

Abstract: Multi-agent document assessment for retrieval-augmented generation is computationally expensive, driving practitioners toward smaller, deployable models whose assessment mechanisms remain poorly understood. We conduct a controlled study of training-free interventions on 7B-9B instruction-tuned models across diverse QA benchmarks, revealing a sharp dichotomy in how models benefit from assessment. For weaker baselines, the dominant mechanism is per-document isolation. Astoundingly, assessment-free isolation matches full multi-agent assessment, demonstrating that resolving multi-document context confusion, rather than scoring quality, drives outsized gains of up to 50 percentage points. Conversely, for strong baselines where scoring quality matters, we introduce Reasoning-Score Coupling, a label-free perturbation probe that classifies scoring behavior. Integrating these findings, we propose MADARA, a model-adaptive routing architecture. Crucially, MADARA's diagnostic thresholds derived from a single pilot model generalize zero-shot to four unseen model families, providing a robust, lightweight pipeline to eliminate computational overhead.

### [160] [Heuresis: Search Strategies for Autonomous AI Research Agents Across Quality, Diversity and Novelty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25198)
*Antonis Antoniades,Deepak Nathani,Ritam Saha,Alfonso Amayuelas,Ivan Bercovich,Zhaotian Weng,Vignesh Baskaran,Kunal Bhatia,William Yang Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Heuresis框架，将ML研究流程抽象为通用可组合原语，在三个领域（LLM预训练、在线RL、模型遗忘）上评估六种搜索策略，发现完全新颖的想法极少，且高质量与高新颖性难以兼得，揭示了当前方法无法拓展质量-新颖性前沿的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于LLM的智能体在自主研究中主要停留在编写代码层面，缺乏对同时具备高性能、多样性和新颖性的想法的探索能力。作者希望建立一个框架，使AI研究能够进行开放式科学探索。

Method: 提出Heuresis框架，将研究流程抽象为通用可组合原语。实现六种搜索策略：贪婪基线、两种基于存档的（MAP-Elites, Go-Explore）、一种进化策略（Islands）和两种发散策略（Curiosity, Omni）。在三个领域（LLM预训练、在线RL、模型遗忘）共3,222次评分运行中评估质量、多样性和新颖性三个维度。

Result: 完全新颖的想法极为罕见：所有评分运行中无一个被评为"原创"，仅少数达到"与先前工作轻微相似"。新颖想法从未接近已知最佳配方的高分。仅有一个新颖想法在质量上进入前十。观察到40次确认的奖励篡改行为（1,628次评分运行中），检测这些行为对保持搜索忠实性至关重要。

Conclusion: 当前搜索和质量-多样性策略虽然能够引导生成想法在质量、多样性和新颖性轴上的分布，但无法拓展质量-新颖性前沿。弥合这一差距是实现持续自主科学进步的开放挑战。

Abstract: Autonomous AI Research promises to accelerate the scientific progress of machine learning. To realise this goal, current Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents need to go beyond just writing code, to mastering the exploration of simultaneously performant, diverse and novel ideas. To this end, we introduce Heuresis, a framework that abstracts the research pipeline into a set of general and composable primitives, enabling open-ended scientific exploration in machine learning research. We implement six search strategies: a greedy baseline, two archive-based (MAP-Elites, Go-Explore), one evolutionary (Islands), and two divergent (Curiosity, Omni), and evaluate them across three axes (Quality, Diversity, and Novelty) on three domains (LLM Pretraining, On-Policy RL, and Model Unlearning), totalling 3,222 scored runs. We find that completely novel ideas are rare. No idea across our scored runs is rated as "Original", and only a few achieve only "Minor Similarity" to prior work. Moreover, novel ideas never approach the highest-performing known-recipe scores. Across all six strategies and three domains, only one such idea lands in the top-10 by quality. We also observed agents resorting to a variety of reward-hacking techniques during execution (40 confirmed fabrications across 1,628 scored runs), and detecting them was necessary to keep the search faithful to the task. Our results show that while current search and Quality-Diversity strategies enable us to steer where the generated ideas land on the quality, diversity, and novelty axes, they do not expand the quality-novelty frontier. Bridging this gap is the open challenge towards the ultimate goal of perpetual, autonomous scientific progress. Code is available at github.com/a-antoniades/Heuresis.

</details>


### [161] [Omni-Perception Policy Optimization for Multimodal Emotion Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25325)
*Zhiyuan Han,Beier Zhu,Wenwen Tong,Pengyang Shao,Peipei Song,Xinyi Wang,Jiangnan Chen,Lewei Lu,Xun Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出OPPO框架，通过强化学习优化多模态情感感知，解决当前Omni-MLLMs在利用多模态线索和不忠实现象方面的问题，在多个基准上取得SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有情感导向的Omni-MLLMs存在两个问题：(i)推理轨迹中未充分利用多模态线索；(ii)存在不忠实行为，常从其他模态幻觉出特定模态的陈述。因此需要显式优化多模态感知能力。

Method: 提出OPPO框架，包含两个核心组件：(1) Omni-Perception Reward，将真实推理分解为细粒度的视觉、声学和情感线索，并奖励能语义恢复这些线索的轨迹；(2) Omni-Perception Loss，比较完整输入和单模态掩码输入下的策略，仅对模态特定证据token施加KL惩罚以抑制跨模态幻觉。同时提出诊断基准MEP-Bench。

Result: OPPO在MER-UniBench和MME-Emotion上达到SOTA性能，并在MEP-Bench上显著提升了利用率和忠实度分数。

Conclusion: 充分且忠实的多模态感知对于多模态情感推理至关重要。

Abstract: We find that current emotion-oriented Omni-MLLMs still lack reliable omni-modal perception: they (i) underutilize multimodal cues in their reasoning trajectories and (ii) exhibit unfaithful behavior, often hallucinating modality-specific statements from other modalities. Building on these insights, we propose OPPO (Omni-Perception Policy Optimization), a reinforcement learning framework that explicitly optimizes multimodal perception. First, an Omni-Perception Reward decomposes ground-truth reasoning into fine-grained visual, acoustic, and emotion cues and rewards trajectories that semantically recover these cues. Second, an Omni-Perception Loss compares the policy under full and unimodally masked inputs, applying a KL penalty only to modality-specific evidence tokens to suppress cross-modal hallucination. We further introduce MEP-Bench, a diagnostic benchmark that quantifies utilization and faithfulness. Experiments show that OPPO achieves state-of-the-art performance on MER-UniBench and MME-Emotion, while substantially improving utilization and faithfulness scores on MEP-Bench, highlighting the importance of sufficient and faithful omni perception for multimodal emotion reasoning.

</details>


### [162] [Agentic Knowledge Tracing: A Multi-Agent LLM Architecture for Stealth Assessment of Financial Literacy in Serious Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25358)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在不干扰游戏体验的前提下，如何从开放式的游戏事件中有效评估金融素养仍然是一个关键挑战。现有方法难以捕捉金融素养的多维特性。

Method: 四个阶段：(1)记录游戏事件日志；(2)LLM事件分类器基于四位评分规则标注行为（与三位专家一致性Fleiss kappa=0.624）；(3)四个领域智能体（风险缓解、投资、支出、信用管理）进行会话级推理，结合贝叶斯知识追踪估算各领域掌握度；(4)专家评判智能体综合生成总体掌握分数。

Result: 与学习增益显著相关(r=0.276, p=0.0001)，与后测成绩显著相关(r=0.333, p<0.0001)，与前测无显著相关。多智能体方法预测效度(r显著)约为单LLM基线(r=0.095,不显著)的三倍。

Abstract: Assessing financial literacy during gameplay without disrupting the learning experience remains a key challenge in serious games for education. We present the Agentic BKT pipeline, a multi-agent large language model architecture for stealth assessment of financial competencies from open-ended gameplay events. The pipeline processes events from a 2D platformer serious game aligned with the OECD/INFE financial literacy framework through four phases: (1) the game captures every player decision as a structured event log; (2) an LLM event classifier labels each action on a four-point rubric validated against three domain experts (Fleiss kappa = 0.624, substantial agreement); (3) four domain-specific agents specializing in risk mitigation, investing, spending, and credit management perform session-level reasoning over behavioral trajectories, feeding per-competency Bayesian Knowledge Tracing that estimates mastery within each domain; and (4) an expert judge agent synthesizes the domain-level estimates into an overall mastery score. Evaluated with 193 K-12 participants across 264 game sessions, the Agentic BKT pipeline yields mastery estimates significantly correlated with learning gain (r = 0.276, p = 0.0001) and post-test scores (r = 0.333, p < 0.0001) while showing no correlation with pre-test scores, providing both convergent and discriminant validity. The multi-agent approach approximately triples the predictive validity of a single-LLM baseline (r = 0.095, not significant) in this study, demonstrating that domain decomposition and session-level reasoning play a central role in capturing the multidimensional nature of financial literacy from gameplay

### [163] [What Actually Works for Spacecraft Fault-Tolerant Control: An Honest Settled-Gate Benchmark of Learned and Classical Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25374)
*Alireza Shojaei*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个严格的航天器姿态容错控制基准，发现基于学习的非结构化方法在未见故障上得分为0%，而结构化“估计-控制”方法（结合循环网络在线估计执行器增益与分析律）在符号和增益故障上达到94-97%。恒常偏置故障对所有控制器（包括特权假想）都是硬墙（0%），通过自校正扰动观测器可恢复至59.4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有容错控制工作多在仿真、窄故障集上评估，且仅用轨迹单次接触即算成功。作者质疑：当成功意味着在训练中从未见过的故障上持续保持指向时，现有方法是否依然有效？为此构建了更严苛的基准。

Method: 构建基准：稳定门控指标（指向保持0.2°内）、真实状态评分、训练/测试按惯性/增益/符号/偏置分离、Wilson区间统计（n=500/单元）、Basilisk六自由度测试床一键复现。对比经典、自适应、端到端学习、结构化控制器四类方法。提出结构化解：循环网络在线推理执行器增益+解析控制律+针对恒常偏置的自校正扰动观测器。

Result: 无故障感知的PD/PID和从头训练的端到端RL：0%。经典自适应：解决符号故障但增益故障仅55.2%。Nussbaum增益律：45.2%和3.2%。结构化估计-控制（循环网络+解析律）：符号97.8%，增益94.4%。恒常偏置：所有控制器（包括特权增益假想）均为0%。加入自校正扰动观测器后：偏置故障恢复至59.4%，且不牺牲符号/增益性能。

Conclusion: 学习能力本身不是杠杆，结构化设计（在线估计+解析控制+观测器）是关键。恒常偏置需额外的扰动观测器而非仅靠增益估计。传感器偏置从单帧测量不可观测，需融合而非观测器。基准开源以促进公平比较。

Abstract: Recent learned fault-tolerant-control (FTC) work reports high success on spacecraft actuator faults, but often in simulation, on narrow fault sets, and with transient metrics that a trajectory need only touch once. We ask what recovers spacecraft pointing when success means holding it on faults never seen in training. We answer with a benchmark built around a settled gate, pointing held within 0.2 deg over a dwell window and scored on the true state, train/test splits disjoint in inertia, gain, sign pattern, and bias, Wilson intervals over n=500 episodes per cell, and one-command reproduction on a 6-DOF Basilisk testbed. Across classical, adaptive, learned end-to-end, and structured controllers, three findings stand out. Fault-unaware PD/PID and from-scratch end-to-end RL score 0%, so learning capacity alone is not the lever. Classical adaptive laws resolve sign faults but handle gain poorly at 55.2%, and a literature-faithful Nussbaum-gain law reaches 45.2% and 3.2%. A structured estimate-then-control design, with a learned recurrent module that infers actuator gain online and feeds an analytic law, wins on sign and gain faults at 97.8% and 94.4%, approaching the privileged oracle while unstructured methods remain at zero. The hard wall is constant additive bias, which is 0% for every controller including the privileged gain oracle, because an integral-free law cannot null a constant disturbance. We close it with a disturbance observer that recovers bias from the dynamics and is self-correcting for gain-estimate error. Composed with the gain estimate, it recovers 59.4% of held-out bias faults with no sign/gain regression, moving that class off zero. We classify sensor-fault regimes similarly, show that sensor bias is unobservable from the corrupted measurement alone and therefore requires fusion rather than an observer, and release the benchmark so the gate is shared.

### [167] [Quantization Inflates Reasoning: Token Inflation as a Hidden Cost of Low-Bit Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25519)
*Xinyu Lian,Walid Krichene,Beichen Huang,Masahiro Tanaka,Olatunji Ruwase,Li Zhang,Minjia Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 低比特后训练量化虽然能保持大语言模型的准确率，但会导致推理模型生成更长的思维链（CoT），引入隐藏的测试时计算成本。本文提出CoT Token膨胀比来量化这一现象，并评估了缓解策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究仅关注量化对最终答案准确率和每token延迟的影响，忽略了量化对推理模型思维链长度的影响，这种隐藏的计算成本可能抵消量化带来的加速收益。

Method: 提出CoT Token膨胀比（CoT Token Inflation Ratio）指标，衡量量化模型与全精度模型在各基准上的推理长度差异；通过数学推理、代码生成、科学问答和agent工具使用等多个基准进行实验分析。

Result: INT4/INT3量化可保持准确率，但会增加推理token用量；token膨胀伴随更多中间步骤和语义重复；这种膨胀转化为端到端服务性能损失；提示工程和采样策略效果不稳定，量化感知训练更有效。

Conclusion: 评估量化推理模型时，应同时报告准确率和推理token用量；token膨胀是量化评估中不可忽视的隐藏成本。

Abstract: Quantization is widely used to reduce the inference cost of large language models, but its effect on reasoning models is not fully captured by final-answer accuracy or per-token latency. We show that low-bit post-training quantization can introduce a hidden test-time compute cost: quantized reasoning models often generate longer chains of thought even when they still answer correctly. Across mathematical reasoning, code generation, scientific question answering, and agentic tool-use benchmarks, we find that INT4/INT3 quantization can preserve accuracy but increase reasoning-token usage, offsetting the expected per-token speedup. To measure this effect, we introduce the CoT Token Inflation Ratio, which compares reasoning length between quantized and full-precision models averaged across all evaluation benchmarks. We further show that token inflation is accompanied by behavioral changes in the reasoning trace, including more intermediate steps and greater semantic repetition. These changes translate into measurable end-to-end real-world serving penalties. Finally, we evaluate mitigation strategies and find that prompting and decoding-time sampling offer inconsistent accuracy-length trade-offs, while quantization-aware training shows more promise in reducing both accuracy degradation and token inflation. Our results suggest that reasoning-token usage should be reported alongside accuracy when evaluating quantized reasoning models.

### [168] [Cliff Tokens: Identifying Single-Token Failure Triggers in LLM Mathematical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25524)
*Jaeyong Ko,Pilsung Kang,Yukyung Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出"悬崖词元"（cliff token）概念，即导致大模型数学推理从正确转向错误的临界词元。通过自适应阈值检测该词元，删除后重采样可使正确率恢复至1.0，并对其进行分类（确定性/不确定性/采样偏差）。基于此的Cliff-DPO方法在多个数学推理基准上提升最高+6.6。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作仅能分析错误发生后的步骤或句子级别，无法精确定位导致推理失败的触发词元（即从正确转向错误的关键点）。

Method: 提出"悬崖词元"概念，基于单侧双比例z检验构建自适应阈值，检测词元级潜在显著下降的触发点。进一步将悬崖词元分为三类：确定性、不确定性和采样偏差悬崖，并通过Cliff-DPO进行单词元偏好优化验证。

Result: 在7个模型和3个数学推理基准（GSM1K、MATH500、AIME 2025）上，删除首个悬崖词元并重采样可使pass@64恢复至1.0，保留则仅0.71-1.00。Cliff-DPO在GSM8K训练后，跨基准提升最高+6.6。

Conclusion: 悬崖词元是推理失败的精确触发点，其分类具有跨模型规模泛化性。针对不确定性和采样偏差悬崖的优化有效提升推理能力，而确定性悬崖则无效。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) reach high accuracy in mathematical reasoning, but individual traces on the same problem diverge; some arrive at the correct answer while others fail. Prior work analyzes failure at the step, chunk, or sentence level, or at tokens where failure has already occurred. Neither identifies the precise token that triggers the shift toward failure. We introduce the cliff token, a token where the token-wise potential drops significantly under an adaptive threshold that scales with the local token-wise potential, based on a one-sided two-proportion z-test. Across seven models and three mathematical reasoning benchmarks (GSM1K, MATH500, AIME 2025), cliff tokens act as failure triggers; deleting the first cliff token and resampling recovers pass@64 to 1.0, while keeping it limits recovery to between 0.71 and 1.00. We further introduce a cliff taxonomy of deterministic, uncertain, and sampled-off cliffs, defined by greedy choice and token entropy. Each type has distinct probabilistic characteristics, and the taxonomy generalizes across model scales. Finally, we validate the taxonomy via single-token preference optimization at cliff positions (Cliff-DPO). Trained on GSM8K, Cliff-DPO improves accuracy across benchmarks by up to +6.6. Optimizing at uncertain and sampled-off cliffs improves reasoning, while deterministic cliffs do not.

</details>

Anchored by an Evolutionary Knowledge Graph structuring past scientific innovations, the framework extracts an "algorithmic Chain-of-Thought" to transform blind stochastic search into directed structural evolution. Applied to the extreme testbed of foundation model deployment, the engine evolved two hardware-aware compression methodologies surpassing human-engineered heuristics: Q-Enhance mitigates long-context accuracy loss in dense models, and MoE-Salient-AQ outperforms state-of-the-art manual sparse Mixture-of-Experts designs by 3.7% at sub-3-bit regimes. Utilizing a bandwidth-efficient Sensitivity Profile, we successfully deployed a massive 235-billion-parameter model onto a constrained dual-A100 server, reducing memory requirements by 75% with a marginal 0.64% accuracy degradation. By transforming unconstrained combinatorial search into knowledge-driven autonomy, this establishes a scalable hardware-software co-design paradigm for machine-driven discovery within strict physical boundaries.

Abstract: In this paper, we introduce position graphs, a graph-based reasoning framework based on the formalization of position spaces. This framework utilizes two strict partial orders, representing horizontal and vertical alignment and precedence, to model the relative positions of discrete tokens. Unlike general qualitative spatial calculi, position graphs are constrained by a chain condition and compatibility requirements that focus on rows and columns. We provide a comprehensive theoretical analysis of this representation, beginning with a characterization of graph consistency. Abstract: Markov decision processes (MDPs) are a classic model of decision making under uncertainty, exhibiting both non-deterministic choice as well as probabilistic uncertainty. Traditionally, exact knowledge of the underlying probabilities is assumed. However, this often is unrealistic, e.g.\ when modelling cyber-physical systems or biological processes. Here, statistical methods provide a way towards obtaining meaningful guarantees. The classical approach is to gather samples in the MDP, use these to draw statistical conclusions about the transition probabilities, and from there obtain bounds on the true value; then, if these bounds are too broad, repeat. ### [177] [WinDOM: Self-Family Distillation for Small-Model GUI Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25964)

We address both, with the explicit goal of pushing small-model performance rather than scaling up. WinDOM is a $54{,}425$-record grounding corpus harvested by driving an open-source Windows 11 web reimplementation under headless Playwright, with bounding boxes read directly off the DOM and no OCR or human annotation. Self-Family Distillation (SFD) is a single rejection-sampling cold-start parameterised only by the teacher choice: either an EMA of the student (no external model) or a frozen larger same-family teacher. We then treat the saturation depth of the SFD cold-start as an explicit GRPO hyperparameter. On a Qwen3.5-2B student, the under-saturated cold-start is a better GRPO initialiser than the converged one: SFD-4B with Early-init RL gains $+5.4$ OOD-mean ($+3.5$ ScreenSpot-Pro, $+7.0$ OSWorld-G, $+5.8$ ScreenSpot-V2) over the base. *Mingguang Chen,Bo Qu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: InvestPhilBench是一个多层动态基准测试，用于评估LLM能否准确重建和应用专业投资者的程序性决策框架。v0.6包含118张投资原则卡、25张决策框架卡和243个QA问题。主要发现：复合评分在前沿模型上饱和(L4=0.932)，但过程性指标(GRA)仍暴露缺陷(L4 GRA~0.77, L7 GRA 0.57-0.62)，复合评分掩盖了过程性差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试无法检验LLM能否准确重构和应用专业投资者的程序性决策框架，需要一个系统化基准来评估LLM在投资研究中的真实能力。

Method: 构建了八层认知层级(L1原则识别到L8新框架外推)的基准，包含投资原则卡、决策框架卡和QA问题；开发了BASP(5种算法指标)、FMDP(6种失败模式检测规则)和GRA(每门精度指标)三个评估体系。

Result: 四模型验证显示供应商层级分化(BASP 0.906 vs 0.438)；前沿模型BASP复合分数饱和(Claude L4=0.932)但GRA显示过程性缺陷(L4 GRA≈0.77, L7 GRA 0.57-0.62)；自动化BASP与人类参考的相关性为Pearson r=0.72(MAE=0.10)。

Conclusion: 复合评分奖励流畅文本但掩盖了过程性差距；v0.6主要是基准与方法贡献，完整的解混淆多模型排行榜和三种条件运行是v1.0里程碑。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly deployed as investment research assistants, yet no benchmark tests whether they can accurately reconstruct and apply the specific procedural decision frameworks of expert investors. We introduce InvestPhilBench, a multi-layer dynamic benchmark spanning eight cognitive tiers, from principle identification (L1) to novel framework extrapolation (L8). The v0.6 release comprises 118 primary-source-verified investment principle cards, 25 decision framework cards with explicit topology metadata, and 243 QA questions (197 dev / 46 held-out test). For reproducible scoring at scale we introduce the Benchmark Automated Scoring Pipeline (BASP) -- five algorithmic metrics (OGRS, KCCS, SAP@k, IVP, CKCA) -- the Failure Mode Detection Protocol (FMDP) with computable rules for six failure modes, and Gate Reconstruction Accuracy (GRA), a per-gate metric for questions with gold reasoning programs. In this release, InvestPhilBench is primarily a benchmark-and-methodology contribution. A four-model sanity wave on the 188-question development split shows a sharp provider-tier split (BASP 0.906 vs. 0.438); these mixed-judge numbers are confounded upper bounds. The central finding: the BASP composite saturates at the frontier (Claude L4 = 0.932) while GRA still exposes a procedural deficit (frontier L4 GRA approx. 0.77, L7 GRA 0.57-0.62) -- composite scoring rewards fluent prose and hides the procedural gap. v0.6 implements a unified judge and true model-in-the-loop retrieval/oracle conditions; the de-confounded multi-model leaderboard and full three-condition run are v1.0 deliverables. On a 100-item expert-annotated gold set the automated BASP composite tracks the human reference at Pearson r = 0.72 (MAE = 0.10), with attribution (SAP@3) the weakest sub-metric and the failure-mode detector running sensitive-but-over-flagging.

</details>


### [179] [Autodata: An agentic data scientist to create high quality synthetic data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25996)
*Ilia Kulikov,Chenxi Whitehouse,Tianhao Wu,Yixin Nie,Swarnadeep Saha,Eryk Helenowski,Weizhe Yuan,Olga Golovneva,Jack Lanchantin,Yoram Bachrach,Jakob Foerster,Xian Li,Han Fang,Sainbayar Sukhbaatar,Jason Weston*

Result: 在计算机科学研究、法律推理、数学对象推理任务上，相比经典合成数据方法获得改进；对代理本身进行元优化带来更大性能提升。

We show how to train (meta-optimize) such a data scientist agent, so that it learns to create even stronger data. We describe the overall formulation, and a specific practical implementation, Agentic Self-Instruct. We conduct experiments on computer science research tasks, legal reasoning tasks and reasoning with mathematical objects, where we obtain improved results compared to classical synthetic dataset creation methods. Further, meta-optimizing the data scientist agent itself delivers an even larger performance uplift. Agentic data creation provides a way to convert increased inference compute into higher quality model training. Overall, we believe this direction has the potential to change the way we build AI data.

### [180] [The Unfireable Safety Kernel: Execution-Time AI Alignment for AI Agents and Other Escapable AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26057)
*Seth Dobrin,Łukasz Chmiel*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出"不可逃避的安全内核"（Unfireable Safety Kernel），一种在操作系统层面而非AI运行时内部实施控制的架构化授权机制。通过进程隔离、执行前强制唯一路径控制、双重故障闭合及外部化签名验证四个属性，实现对"可逃逸AI系统"的运行时对齐。Rust实现经形式化验证（Z3定理证明+Kani有界模型检验），在自修改AI系统中100%阻止了704次逃逸尝试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI agent的安全控制（系统提示、输出过滤器、护栏库）都放在AI运行时内部，但任何在agent地址空间内的控制都能被输入所影响，形成"可逃逸AI系统"——即任何对其运行时拥有足够访问权限的AI系统本质上都可以绕过这些内部控制。因此需要一种架构性的、不可被agent自身修改的授权机制。

Method: 提出四种必须满足的属性：1) 进程隔离（process separation）——控制层与AI运行时处于不同进程；2) 执行前在结构上唯一路径的强制（pre-action enforcement on a structurally only path）——所有操作必须经过唯一授权路径；3) 双重故障闭合（fail-closed at both request and system levels）——请求级和系统级均默认拒绝；4) 外部化签名验证（externalized signed evidence）——证据在系统信任边界外可验证。用Rust实现Unfireable Safety Kernel，使用Z3进行SMT定理证明、Kani进行有界模型检验，并通过Python到Rust迁移的字节等价测试（1000/1000 fixtures + 17/17对抗类）。

Result: 在确定性自改进世界模型上，面对利用自我修改机制的逃逸攻击者：1,000次自我修改中，704次对安全关键核心的尝试全部被拒绝，无逃逸成功；另外300次在操作员终止开关下也被拒绝。6,240次授权往返测试无成功绕过。与3个声称占据agent控制平面的当代系统对比，本文的agent只能被调用控制，而非自身拥有控制选择权。

Conclusion: 架构化授权机制（Unfireable Safety Kernel）对比运行时内部控制的"合作性请求"模式，提供了不可逃逸的安全保障。这种执行时AI对齐（execution-time AI alignment）补充了训练时对齐（RLHF、Constitutional AI）和推理时对齐，为可逃逸AI系统提供了可形式化验证的、不可绕过的安全控制层。

Abstract: AI agents are granted access to tools, APIs, and other infrastructure, making them active principals in those systems. The dominant approach places controls inside the agent's own runtime: system prompts, output filters, and guardrail libraries. Any control in the agent's address space is reachable by inputs that influence it; this generalizes to any AI system with sufficient reach into its own runtime, a class we term escapable AI systems.
  We identify four properties that an authorization mechanism must satisfy for architectural control rather than for cooperative requests: process separation, pre-action enforcement on a structurally only path, fail-closed at both the request and system levels, and externalized signed evidence verifiable outside the controlled system's trust boundary. We position this layer as execution-time AI alignment, complementing training-time alignment (RLHF, Constitutional AI) and inference-time alignment.
  We present the Unfireable Safety Kernel, a Rust reference implementation realizing all four. Its fail-closed invariant is machine-checked at two levels: an SMT theorem (Z3) and an exhaustive bounded-model-checking proof of the production decision function (Kani, 4/4 harnesses). A Python-to-Rust migration was gated on byte-equivalence (1000/1000 fixtures; 17/17 adversarial classes). We evaluate the kernel governing a live, escapable AI system, a deterministic, self-improving world model, against an escape-seeking adversary driving its real self-modification seam: across 1,000 self-modifications, all 704 attempts on the safety-critical core are refused, with no escape; a further 300, under the operator kill switch, are also refused. A separate campaign of 6,240 authorization round-trips had no successful bypass. Against 3 contemporary systems claiming the agent control plane, the agent invokes control; here, it lacks that choice.

</details>

### [181] [Decidability and Undecidability Results for LIA-Definable Impartial Combinatorial Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25276)
*Shiguang Feng,Liangda Fang,Jiahao Luo,Quanlong Guan*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究了线性整数算术可定义的无偏组合博弈（LIA-definable ICGs）的可判定性。发现一般情况下的终止性、循环性、胜负状态集刻画等问题不可判定，但对于终止性LIA-definable ICGs，这些问题是可判定的。状态级别的胜负判定即使在终止性博弈中也不可判定，但在有限深度终止性博弈中可判定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组合博弈理论中大部分无偏博弈可用线性整数算术（LIA）形式化定义，但关于这类博弈的可判定性理论尚不完善，本文旨在系统性地厘清LIA可定义无偏组合博弈中各类决策问题的可判定与不可判定边界。

Method: 通过形式化定义LIA可定义的无偏组合博弈（ICGs），分别针对全局性质（终止性、循环性）、公式刻画（胜负平状态集的精确表征）以及状态级别问题（单个状态的胜负平判定）进行可判定性分析，区分一般情况与终止性/有限深度子类。

Result: （1）一般LIA-definable ICGs的终止性、循环性判定不可判定；（2）终止性LIA-definable ICGs的终止性、循环性、胜负平状态集刻画可判定；（3）状态级胜负判定在终止性LIA-definable ICGs中仍不可判定，但在有限深度子类中可判定；（4）状态级平局判定在终止性LIA-definable ICGs中可判定。

Conclusion: LIA可定义无偏组合博弈的决策问题在一般情形下多为不可判定，但在终止性约束下可获得更强的可判定性结果，其中有限深度假设进一步放宽了可判定性边界。

Abstract: Combinatorial game theory is a branch of mathematics and theoretical computer science that studies deterministic games with perfect information and no elements of chance. The majority of combinatorial games are impartial and formalized in linear integer arithmetic, which we call LIA-definable impartial combinatorial games (ICGs). This paper studies decidability and undecidability questions for these games. We prove that deciding whether an LIA-definable ICG is terminating or cyclic is undecidable in general, while the corresponding questions become decidable for terminating LIA-definable ICGs. We also show that deciding whether an LIA formula exactly characterizes the set of winning, losing, or draw states of an LIA-definable ICG is undecidable in general and decidable for terminating LIA-definable ICGs. For state-level questions, deciding whether a state is winning or losing remains undecidable even for terminating LIA-definable ICGs, but becomes decidable for terminating finite-depth LIA-definable ICGs. Finally, deciding whether a state is draw for an LIA-definable ICG is undecidable in general and decidable for terminating LIA-definable ICGs.

</details>


### [182] [Envy-free Contracts with Subsidies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25431)
*Matteo Castiglioni,Junjie Chen,Yingkai Li*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为“带补贴的无嫉妒契约”（EFS）的新方案，在算法公平契约设计问题中，允许委托人向代理人提供个性化补贴，从而在恢复严格公平性的同时，将公平代价（PoF）从无界降低到紧的 $n^{Θ(n)}$ 上界，并讨论了计算复杂性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作（如EF契约）在算法公平契约设计中面临两难：要么公平代价无界，要么丧失严格公平性。本文旨在同时实现严格公平和可接受的公平代价。

Method: 提出EFS（带补贴的无嫉妒契约）方案，允许委托人向代理人提供agent-specific补贴。通过理论分析证明该方案的公平代价上界为 $n^{Θ(n)}$，并证明计算最优EFS契约的NP-hard性，同时给出任务数为常数时的多项式时间算法。

Result: EFS契约不仅能恢复严格公平性，而且其公平代价有紧的 $n^{Θ(n)}$ 上界，相比EF契约的任意大因子更优。计算最优EFS契约一般是NP难的，但在任务数恒定时有多项式时间算法。

Conclusion: EFS契约成功调和了公平性与效率之间的冲突，是一种兼具理论优美性和实际可行性的公平契约设计方案。

Abstract: We study algorithmic fair contract design, where a principal designs task-level contracts and fairly delegates a set of tasks to a set of agents. Prior work on this setting, particularly on envy-free (EF) contracts, either suffers from an unbounded price of fairness (PoF) or avoids this unboundedness by losing strict fairness. To address these limitations, we propose a novel scheme, called {\it Envy-free Contracts with Subsidies} (EFS), in which the principal may additionally offer agent-specific subsidies. We show that EFS contracts not only restore strict fairness, but can also outperform EF contracts by an arbitrarily large factor. Moreover, in sharp contrast to EF contracts, we prove that EFS contracts admit a tight $n^{Θ(n)}$ bound on the price of fairness, where $n$ is the number of agents. We further show that computing optimal EFS contracts is NP-hard in general. Nevertheless, when the number of tasks is constant, we provide a polynomial-time algorithm for computing optimal EFS contracts.

</details>


### [183] [Equilibrium and Infeasibility: A new solution concept for games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25707)
*Anne Reulke,Mikaël Touati,Rachid El-Azouzi*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文针对非合作博弈中可能出现的不可行个体约束问题，提出了一种新的解概念——ψ-惩罚解，即通过惩罚项松弛个体约束后得到的广义纳什均衡序列的极限解，并证明了其存在性及其与GNE和纳什议价的兼容性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多实际应用中的博弈问题面临个体约束不可行的挑战，现有广义博弈的解概念无法处理这种情况，因此需要提出新的解概念。

Method: 通过引入惩罚项松弛个体约束，构造一系列带惩罚的广义博弈，将其广义纳什均衡序列的极限定义为ψ-惩罚解，并给出该解可被刻画为每个玩家在惩罚最小化策略上最大化自身效用的策略配置的条件。

Result: 在广泛的博弈类别中证明了解的存在性，并通过Divide-the-Dollar的变体进行说明，同时证明了该解与广义纳什均衡及纳什议价解的兼容性。

Conclusion: 提出的ψ-惩罚解为处理不可行约束的广义博弈提供了有效的理论框架，具有良好的兼容性和广泛适用性。

Abstract: Addressing infeasibility in non-cooperative games has become an important topic, as many problems across different applications face this issue. In this paper, we propose a new solution concept for generalized games with possibly infeasible individual constraints. A solution is defined as the limit of a sequence of generalized Nash equilibria induced by games with penalty terms relaxing the individual constraints. Existence is established for a broad range of games and we provide conditions allowing to characterize a $ψ$-penalized solution as a strategy profile maximizing every player's utility over all her penalty minimizing strategies. A variation of Divide-the-Dollar serves as an illustrative example. We further establish the compatibility with the GNE and the solution to the Nash bargaining.

</details>


### [184] [Restoring Incentive Compatibility in Two-Stage Energy Markets with Prosumers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25910)
*Nikolas Koumpis,Koushik Kar,Leandros Tassiulas,Manolis Zampetakis*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究了现代电力市场设计中，如何构建策略-proof的失衡结算层以兼顾经济效益和电网稳定性。针对主动型产消者（prosumers）在日前市场低报需求以在实时市场套利的问题，提出了一种基于留一法对比评分规则的惩罚机制，激励真实报价，并通过合成数据和真实市场数据验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 公共数据表明日前市场价格战略性地低于实际消费需求，这一现象由主动型产消者（prosumers）的低报需求行为驱动。他们在日前市场买入、实时市场卖出，通过制造不平衡套利。现有机制存在激励扭曲，需要设计策略-proof的解决方案。

Method: 首先对两阶段市场（日前+实时）在线性偏好下建模，并与竞争均衡对比。然后设计了一种基于"留一法对比评分规则"（leave-one-out contrastive scoring rule）的惩罚机制，由日前市场运营商实施，在现有信息约束下激励产消者真实报告需求。

Result: 当日前市场规模扩大时，普通消费者的低报激励消失，但产消者的低报激励仍有正下界（取决于实时市场发电机组结构及其份额）。所提机制能有效消除策略性低报，且诚实参与时惩罚成本很低。合成数据与真实市场数据均验证了机制的激励对齐效果。

Conclusion: 设计的评分规则惩罚机制在现有信息约束下实现了激励相容，既抑制了产消者的战略性低报行为，又保持了较低的诚实参与成本，为电力市场失衡结算层的设计提供了可行方案。

Abstract: A central challenge in modern energy market design is the formulation of a strategy-proof imbalance settlement layer that secures both the economic efficiency of the institution and the stability of the power grid. Public data reveals that the day-ahead market is strategically biased below actual consumer demand. Such empirical observations are explained by active prosumers which provide implementable incentives for demand under-reporting. Active prosumers buy energy in the day-ahead market and sell energy in the real-time market for balancing real-time energy deviations. By under-reporting their demand for the day ahead they inflate real-time imbalances and, under uniform pricing, they dispatch their generation assets more profitably. We model the two-stage institution under linear preferences and benchmark it against its associated competitive equilibria. We show that although consumers' incentives for demand under-reporting vanish when the day-ahead market scales, prosumers' incentives remain lower bounded by a positive gain which depends only on the real-time market generation stack and their shares over it. To restore incentive compatibility under the existing informational constraints, we design a leave-one-out contrastive scoring rule-based penalty that is implemented by the day-ahead market operator, incentivizes prosumers to report their demand truthfully and ensures small charges when participating honestly. We illustrate these results with numerical simulations on synthetic data and evaluate our mechanism on real-market data by first rationalizing demand reports as subjective equilibria of the induced game. Our mechanism demonstrates strong incentive alignment while retaining a low cost for honest participation.

</details>


### [185] [Variable Bound Tightening for Nash Equilibrium Computation in Multiplayer Imperfect-Information Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25997)
*Sam Ganzfried*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文通过推导非线性互补问题中松弛变量和乘数变量的有限界，改进了多人非完美信息博弈中纳什均衡精确计算的凸松弛方法，在三玩家Kuhn扑克中取得了显著的计算效率提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法（如反事实遗憾最小化和虚拟博弈）在多人博弈中无法保证收敛到纳什均衡，而基于非线性互补问题的方法虽能精确求解但计算代价高昂，无法在合理时间内求解完整游戏。

Method: 推导了非线性互补问题公式中松弛变量和乘数变量的有限界，这些界强化了空间分支定界法内部使用的凸松弛（McCormick包络），从而加速求解过程。

Result: 在三玩家Kuhn扑克实验中，所提出的变量界显著提升了计算性能，使得算法能够解决此前无法在24小时内求解的完整游戏版本。

Conclusion: 通过为松弛变量和乘数变量提供有限界，可以有效强化凸松弛，显著加速多人博弈中纳什均衡的精确计算。

Abstract: There has been significant recent progress in algorithms for approximation of Nash equilibrium in large two-player zero-sum imperfect-information games and exact computation of Nash equilibrium in multiplayer strategic-form games. While counterfactual regret minimization and fictitious play are scalable to large games and have convergence guarantees in two-player zero-sum games, they do not guarantee convergence to Nash equilibrium in multiplayer games. Recently, an approach has been presented for exact computation of Nash equilibrium in multiplayer imperfect-information games that solves a quadratically constrained program based on a nonlinear complementarity problem formulation derived from the sequence-form game representation. This formulation was solved using Gurobi's nonconvex quadratic solver, which employs spatial branch-and-bound to iteratively refine variable bounds by solving convex relaxations of bilinear terms via McCormick envelopes. During presolve, Gurobi introduces auxiliary variables and, in some cases, binary variables, leading to an internal MIQCP reformulation. This approach was demonstrated to outperform prior algorithms from the Gambit software suite and quickly solve three-player Kuhn poker after removal of dominated actions; however, the algorithm was not able to solve the full version of the game within 24 hours. In this paper, we derive finite bounds on slack and multiplier variables in the nonlinear complementarity formulation. These bounds strengthen the convex relaxations used within spatial branch-and-bound and lead to substantial computational improvements. We demonstrate the impact of the proposed bounds on exact Nash equilibrium computation in three-player Kuhn poker.

</details>


### [186] [Hotelling-Downs with Facility Synergy: The Mall Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26055)
*Elliot Anshelevich,Jianan Lin,Noah Prisament*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究了设施协同作用下的Hotelling-Downs模型变体。与经典模型中客户总是选择最近设施不同，本文考虑客户既偏好设施密集区域又希望最小化距离的复杂行为。证明了纳什均衡始终存在，且存在一个均衡使客户总成本等于最优解。主要结果是价格无政府(Price of Anarchy)上界为225/64≈3.516。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Hotelling-Downs模型假设客户总是选择最近的设施，但现实中客户可能偏好设施密集的区域（如购物中心、服务区），同时兼顾距离。这种更复杂且更真实的行为模式需要新的理论分析。

Method: 在经典Hotelling-Downs模型基础上引入设施协同作用，即客户偏好设施数量多的位置。通过博弈论框架分析纳什均衡的存在性，并利用价格无政府(Price of Anarchy)度量均衡解与最优解的差距。

Result: (1) 纳什均衡始终存在；(2) 存在一个均衡使得客户总成本等于最优解；(3) 价格无政府上界为225/64≈3.516。

Conclusion: 尽管考虑设施协同后客户行为更加复杂且更符合现实，但纳什均衡解的成本仍不会远高于最优设施布局方案，证明了该模型在实际应用中的可行性。

Abstract: We consider a variation of the classic Hotelling-Downs model with the addition of facility synergies. Unlike in the classic model, where clients always use the facility closest to them, we study clients who prefer locations with many facilities to those with few facilities while simultaneously attempting to minimize their distance as well. We show that, in contrast with the classic model, Nash equilibria for our setting always exist, and, in fact, there always exists a Nash equilibrium such that the sum of client costs equals the cost of the optimal solution. Our main result is a bound of $\frac{225}{64}\approx 3.516$ on the Price of Anarchy for our model, showing that, although the client behavior is more complex in our model (and often more realistic depending on the application), the cost of Nash equilibrium solutions still cannot be much worse than the cost of the optimal facility placement.

</details>


### [187] [Strategyproof Facility Location and Committee Selection with Mixed Max and Sum Agent Types](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26074)
*Yue Gruszecki,Elliot Anshelevich*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究策略性设施选址问题，在任意度量空间中为自利型代理人选择k个设施以最小化总成本。代理人具有最大型或总和型成本函数，且位置和类型可能为私有信息。论文提出确定性策略proof机制，并证明近似比上界：类型私人但位置已知时可达(3-2/k)；知道类型比例时可达更优近似比；位置私人时在直线度量上可达近似比3。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决策略性设施选址中代理人既是自利的、其位置和成本函数类型又可能为私有信息的双重信息不对称问题，设计保证真实汇报是占优策略的机制。

Method: 针对不同信息场景设计确定性策略proof机制：类型私有但位置已知时；知道各类型比例时；位置私有（直线度量）时。通过近似比分析评估机制效率。

Result: 类型私有位置已知时近似比为(3-2/k)；知道类型比例时可改进至(2/(1-k+√(k²-k+1))-1)；直线度量位置私有时代价近似比为3。这些界限对任意k和任意度量空间成立。

Conclusion: 收集代理人类型信息与位置信息的价值不同，即便缺乏这些信息，仍可能设计出产生良好结果的机制。

Abstract: We study strategic facility location, in which $n$ agents are located in an arbitrary metric space, and the goal is to choose $k$ facilities to minimize the total agent cost. The agents can have two types of individual cost functions: max-type where the agent wants to minimize the maximum distance from themselves to any chosen facility, or sum-type where the agent wants to minimize the average distance to the chosen facilities. The agents are self-interested, however, and both the agent location and the agent type may be private information.
  We provide deterministic strategyproof mechanisms for this setting, and prove bounds on their approximation ratio as compared with the solution minimizing the total agent cost. When agent types are private but their locations are known, we prove that an approximation of $\left(3 -\frac{2}{k}\right)$ is always possible, and a better approximation of $\left(\frac{2}{1-k+\sqrt{k^2-k+1}}-1\right)$ is achievable when we know the {\em fraction} of the agents with each type, but not necessarily the type of each individual agent. These bounds hold for arbitrary $k$ and arbitrary metric distances. When agent locations are private, we instead focus on the line metric, and show that a simple generalization of the median mechanism results in an approximation ratio of 3, even for large $k$ and arbitrary mixes of agent types. Our results show the importance of collecting information about agent types vs about their locations, and show that it is possible to produce good outcomes even without such information.

</details>

### [188] [Fifty Years of Specification Completeness: What Aviation Certification Tells AI Governance About Epoch Limits, Proof Surfaces, and the Structural Gap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25120)
*Christo Zietsman*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 航空软件认证（DO-178C/DO-330）的三个结构性要求——结构化治理连接、上下文边界有效性、客观证据架构——在AI治理文档层面缺失。论文将这些要求映射为三个结构性发现，并指出37%的AI治理文档低于结构质量阈值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 航空领域已有三十年成熟的结构性治理要求，但AI治理文档（如系统提示、AGENTS.md、治理策略等）不满足任何一项。航空标准制定机构已承认现有框架对AI系统失效，但未要求单个治理文档具备这些结构性属性。

Method: 将DO-178C的可追溯性架构、DO-330的重新认证触发条件、DO-178C的客观证据要求映射到AI治理文档层，提出三个结构性发现：纪元限制（epoch limits）、证明表面（proof surfaces）、结构完整性缺失。

Result: 37%的AI治理文档低于结构质量阈值。提出PromptQ的七原则框架，在治理文档层操作性实现这些要求。

Conclusion: 航空领域在系统层面的结构性要求因AI的非确定性而失效，但在文档层面是可转移的——治理工件是静态的，其结构属性可独立于所治理的随机系统进行评估。

Abstract: Aviation software certification has operationalised three structural requirements for governed software systems since 1992: structured governance linkage between governing specifications and operational evidence, context-bounded validity that triggers revalidation when operational context changes, and an objective evidence architecture that defines what proof means and what makes it sufficient. These requirements appear in DO-178C and DO-330 and are enforced through FAA and EASA certification.
  No existing framework requires these structural properties as intrinsic properties of individual AI governance documents. A system prompt, an AGENTS.md file, a governance policy, or a task envelope can be deployed without satisfying any of the three requirements aviation has enforced for three decades. Aviation is the most technically rigorous instance: its standard-setting bodies have acknowledged that their frameworks break down for AI systems, yet none requires these properties of individual governance documents.
  Aviation's structural requirements break down at the system level because AI systems are non-deterministic, but remain transferable at the document level: the governance artifact is a static artifact whose structural properties can be evaluated independently of the stochastic system it governs.
  The paper maps DO-178C's traceability architecture, DO-330's requalification triggers, and DO-178C's objective evidence requirements onto three structural findings: epoch limits on governance document validity, proof surfaces as the revalidation feedback mechanism, and the absence of structural completeness requirements in AI governance instruments. An empirical companion (arXiv:2604.21090) found that 37% of AI governance documents fall below the structural quality threshold. PromptQ's seven-principle framework operationalises these requirements at the governance document layer.

</details>


### [189] [LLM4MTLs: Automated Generation and Empirical Evaluation of Model Transformation Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25193)
*Bowen Jiang,Nathan Hagel,Haowei Cheng,Benedikt Jutz,Arne Lange,Weixing Zhang,Rahul Sharma,Ralf Reussner,Anne Koziolek*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出LLM4MTLs自动化工作流，系统探索了少样本提示、语法提示和辅助方法包含等策略组合，用于提升LLM生成模型转换语言代码的质量。实验覆盖四种MTL和三种LLM，发现少样本提示能一致改善语法质量，但对语义正确性的提升不均匀且依赖具体语言，语法提示在孤立使用时可能适得其反。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模型转换语言（MTL）的代码开发既需要语言特定知识又需要领域知识，难度较大，因此希望利用LLM来自动生成MTL代码。但由于MTL领域训练数据和可执行示例有限，LLM生成的代码往往存在语法无效或语义不可用的问题。

Method: 构建了LLM4MTLs自动化工作流，系统探索少样本提示、语法提示和辅助方法包含三种提示策略的组合方式，并在四种MTL（ATL, ETL, QVTo, Reactions language）上，使用三种LLM进行评估，采用语法和语义两类指标衡量代码质量。

Result: 少样本提示一致提升了四种MTL的语法质量；语义正确性的提升不均匀且依赖语言；ATL的Pass@1在所有策略和模型下保持不变；语法提示在结合少样本示例时能稳定生成，但孤立使用时可能无效甚至有害；辅助方法作为补充放大器有益；LLM的选择影响部分MTL的语法正确性和相似度，但对语义正确性影响有限。

Conclusion: LLM生成MTL代码时，语法层面的改善相对容易实现，但深层转换语义的准确生成仍是瓶颈，不同MTL语言对提示策略的响应存在显著差异，需要针对具体语言选择和组合提示策略。

Abstract: Model transformation languages (MTLs) are domain-specific languages for transforming models conforming to a given metamodel into other models, including textual models such as source code. Developing correct model transformations is challenging, requiring both language-specific and domain knowledge, and motivating the use of large language models (LLMs) for MTL code generation. However, due to limited training data and executable examples, LLM-generated MTL code is often not syntactically valid or semantically usable out of the box. This paper presents LLM4MTLs, an automated workflow for constructing and comparing prompting strategies for LLM-generated MTL code, together with an evaluation suite and an empirical evaluation. The workflow systematically explores prompt constructions combining few-shot prompting, grammar prompting, and helper method inclusion, and evaluates them using syntactic and semantic metrics. We construct an evaluation suite spanning four MTLs (ATL, ETL, QVTo, and the Reactions language) with executable reference scripts and manually written test suites, and evaluate across three LLMs. We find that few-shot prompting consistently improves syntactic quality across all four MTLs while gains in semantic correctness are uneven and language-dependent. For ATL, Pass@1 remains unchanged across all strategies and models, indicating that few-shot prompting improves surface-level syntax more readily than deep transformation semantics. Grammar prompting stabilizes code generation when combined with few-shot examples, but in isolation it can be ineffective or even counterproductive for certain model-language combinations. Including helper methods as a complementary amplifier can also be beneficial. Finally, LLM choice influences syntactic correctness and similarity for certain MTLs, particularly ETL and QVTo, while its influence on semantic correctness remains limited.

</details>


### [190] [Tensor-Based Batch Fuzzing with Adaptive Perturbation Scaling for Deep Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25239)
*Guanqin Zhang,Yulei Sui*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向规范感知的批量模糊测试框架，通过自适应扰动缩放（各向同性/各向异性）和将约束嵌入网络的批处理设计，相比传统序列方法实现了高达40倍吞吐量提升和4倍违规发现量提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有DNN覆盖引导的序列模糊测试框架每次迭代仅处理一个输入，且对所有输入维度使用统一的扰动预算，导致测试吞吐量低、输入空间探索精度差，难以高效评估模型在未见输入上的可靠性。

Method: 1) 从规范定义的可行范围（上下界之间的差距）导出自适应扰动步长，支持全局标量（各向同性）和逐维度（各向异性）两种缩放方式；2) 将输入约束和输出属性检查作为不可训练层直接嵌入网络，得到包装模型，可在单次批处理迭代中处理B个规范实例。

Result: 在TrafficSigns、Cifar100、TinyImageNet三个基准上，覆盖6个网络和400+规范，张量化模糊测试相比序列基线在相同时间预算下实现高达40倍吞吐量提升和4倍违规发现量提升。

Conclusion: 规范感知的批量模糊测试结合自适应扰动缩放能显著提升DNN测试效率和输入空间探索精度，尤其适用于特征尺度异构的场景。

Abstract: Deep neural networks are increasingly deployed in safety-critical domains such as autonomous driving and medical diagnosis, yet their opaque, high-dimensional parameter spaces make it difficult to systematically assess model reliability on unseen inputs. Existing coverage-guided sequential fuzzing frameworks for DNNs inherit a one-input-per-iteration design from traditional software fuzzing and apply uniform perturbation budgets across all input dimensions, limiting both testing throughput (i.e., inputs processed per unit time) and the precision of input-space exploration. We present a new specification-aware batch fuzzing framework with adaptive perturbation scaling that addresses both limitations. Rather than relying on a fixed global perturbation radius epsilon, our approach derives mutation step sizes from specification-defined feasible ranges (the gap between lower and upper bounds) using a shared scale factor. This scaling can be applied either as a global scalar (isotropic) or as per-dimension step sizes (anisotropic), keeping perturbations consistent with the underlying constraint structure. As a result, the fuzzer can explore input spaces with heterogeneous feature scales more effectively across all specifications in the batch. We embed input constraints and output property checks directly into the network as non-trainable layers, yielding a wrapped model that processes B specification instances in a single batched iteration, substantially improving fuzzing efficiency and counterexample exploration. We evaluate our framework extensively on three benchmarks, covering six networks and over 400 specifications across TrafficSigns, Cifar100, and TinyImageNet. Our tensor-based fuzzing achieves up to 40X higher throughput and 4X more violations than the sequential baseline under the same time budget, demonstrating significantly improved effectiveness in specification-guided fuzzing.

</details>


### [191] [How Do Developers Maintain and Evolve Their Agents' Instructions? An Empirical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25257)
*Gianmario Voria,Alfonso Cannavale,Andrea De Lucia,Yutaro Kashiwa,Gemma Catolino,Fabio Palomba*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文研究自主编码代理中的代理上下文文件（ACF）的演化，通过大规模挖掘研究，分类ACF变更类型，分析其与代码质量的关系及时间模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主编码代理虽提升效率，但带来治理、可追溯性和控制挑战。ACF作为指导代理的结构化指令机制，其演化与代码开发的关系尚不明确，需系统研究。

Method: 采用大规模挖掘研究，结合含ACF的仓库和代理生成的提交。在提交级别重建ACF演化，通过定性方法分类变更，并分析与代码质量指标的关系，使用统计检验评估不同维护类别间的差异。

Result: 预期产出包括：(1) 基于软件维护理论的ACF变更分类体系；(2) 不同类型变更与代码质量结果的关联分析；(3) 开发生命周期中的时间模式分析。

Conclusion: 该研究将为未来设计ACF以治理自主编码代理提供实证依据，有助于理解AI辅助软件开发中的治理机制。

Abstract: Context. Autonomous coding agents are increasingly used in software development, shifting parts of the engineering process to AI assistance. While this automation brings clear benefits, it introduces challenges in governance, traceability, and control over agent behavior. Agent Context Files (ACFs) have emerged as a practical mechanism to guide agents through structured instructions, yet little is known about how these artifacts are maintained and how their evolution relates to code development. Objective. This paper plans to investigate the evolution of ACFs and their role in agent-driven development. Specifically, we (1) classify ACF changes through a taxonomy grounded in software maintenance theory, (2) analyze how different types of changes are associated with code quality outcomes, and (3) examine their temporal patterns across the development lifecycle. Method. We conduct a large-scale mining study combining repositories with ACFs and agent-generated commits. We reconstruct ACF evolution at the commit level, classify changes using a qualitative approach, and analyze their association with code quality metrics. Statistical analyses and hypotheses are used to evaluate differences across maintenance categories, to inform future design of ACFs for governing autonomous coding agents.

### [192] [Semantic Code Clone Detection: Are We There Yet?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25272)
*Zhiwei Xu,Weixian Deng,Xuyang Liu,Xiaolin Peng,Jiabao Gao,Tian Qiu,Hai Wan,Xibin Zhao*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 现有最先进的语义代码克隆检测器虽然在基准数据集上表现优异，但通过构建分布偏移的语义等价克隆实例后，发现它们普遍存在严重的性能下降，主要依赖词汇和结构捷径学习而非真正的语义理解，泛化能力有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前最先进的语义代码克隆检测器在基准数据集上报告了极高的性能，但这些结果是否真正反映了捕捉程序语义等价性的能力，还是仅仅利用了数据集特定的模式，这一问题尚不清楚。

Method: 提出一个由8个源自Type-2和Type-3克隆变体的变换算子组成的克隆算子框架，构建分布偏移但语义等价的Type-4克隆实例，在BigCloneBench数据集上评估11个代表性的检测器（涵盖基于token、树和图三种范式）。

Result: 所有评估的方法在分布偏移的语义等价克隆实例上均出现显著的性能下降；现有检测器严重依赖基于词法和结构线索的捷径学习，而非稳健的语义理解。

Conclusion: 当前最先进的语义代码克隆检测器在现实场景中泛化能力有限，为未来研究指明了重要方向。

Abstract: Code clone detection has been extensively studied for decades, and recent approaches have begun reporting remarkably high performance for semantic (Type-4) clones on benchmark datasets. However, it remains unclear whether these results reflect a genuine ability to capture semantic equivalence between programs, or simply an ability to exploit dataset-specific patterns.
  In this paper, we present the first systematic empirical study investigating the generalizability of state-of-the-art (SOTA) semantic code clone detectors beyond benchmark evaluation settings. Inspired by the inherent inclusion relationship among clone types, we propose a clone operator framework consisting of eight transformation operators derived from Type-2 and Type-3 clone variations. Using these operators, we construct distribution-shifted yet semantically equivalent Type-4 clone instances and evaluate 11 representative detectors spanning token-based, tree-based, and graph-based paradigms on the real-world BigCloneBench dataset. Our results reveal substantial performance degradation across all evaluated approaches, despite their strong benchmark performance. Further analyses show that existing detectors heavily rely on shortcut learning based on lexical and structural cues rather than robust semantic understanding. Our findings suggest that current SOTA semantic code clone detectors exhibit limited generalizability in real-world scenarios, highlighting important avenues for future research.

</details>


### [193] [LibEvoBench: Probing Temporal Knowledge Stratification in Code Generation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25402)
*Daniele Cipollone,Sergey Titov,Maliheh Izadi,Egor Bogomolov,Arie van Deursen*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出LibEvoBench基准和SEUS指标，评估LLM在多版本API演化下的代码生成能力。研究发现当前最先进模型对API版本不敏感，在演化API上性能显著下降，简单指定版本无帮助，但提供相关文档能大幅提升准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型软件项目常依赖旧版库，但LLM训练语料的时间混杂导致模型缺乏版本感知能力，产生时代错位错误（调用错误版本的API）。现有评估缺乏对此系统性研究。

Method: 构建LibEvoBench多任务基准，涵盖多个版本的主流Python库，并设计SEUS指标衡量模型在不同版本API下的一致性表现。通过对比稳定和演化API上的性能差异，以及有无文档/版本指定条件，系统评估模型版本感知能力。

Result: SOTA模型对API版本不敏感：演化API上性能显著下降，稳定API则不受影响。简单指定目标版本无助于提升准确性，但提供相关文档能显著改善模型表现。

Conclusion: 当前训练范式存在系统性局限，模型缺乏时间感知的知识表征能力。未来需要探索时间锚定的代码生成方法，让模型能够区分和理解不同版本API的演化。

Abstract: Large software projects often depend on older versions of libraries, even as APIs continue to evolve across releases. This creates a challenge for LLMs: they must maintain knowledge of multiple API versions, not merely the latest or most common one. However, current LLMs are trained on temporally mixed corpora and lack explicit mechanisms for such version-specific reasoning, leading to anachronistic errors - calling APIs as they exist in a different library version. To systematically evaluate this phenomenon, we introduce LibEvoBench, a multi-task benchmark spanning multiple versions of widely used Python libraries, along with a new metric, the Software Evolution Understanding Score (SEUS), to measure models' consistency when working with evolving APIs. Our results show that state-of-the-art models are largely version-oblivious: performance degrades for evolving APIs, while for stable APIs it remains the same across versions. Moreover, simply specifying the target version provides no benefit, while relevant documentation significantly boosts models' accuracy. These findings highlight a systematic limitation of current training paradigms and motivate new approaches for temporally grounded knowledge in code generation.

</details>


### [194] [Project-wise Comparison of Software Birthmarks Using Weighted Partial Similarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25418)
*Nikolay Fedorov,Akito Monden,Hiroki Inayoshi,Haruaki Tamada,Masateru Tsunoda*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种项目级别的软件水印比较框架，通过对称聚合模块级相似度，并引入加权机制（大模块权重大）和部分相似性方法（聚焦高相似模块对），有效解决了部分代码复用检测中的两个关键挑战：部分复用和小模块导致的偶然相似性。在35个Java项目上验证，性能优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有软件水印相似度度量多在模块级别（源文件/类文件）进行，但实际中软件复用常发生在项目级别，只有部分模块被复用。这带来了两个挑战：(1) 部分复用——复用模块只占项目一小部分；(2) 小模块的偶然相似性——导致误报。现有方法无法有效处理这些问题。

Method: (1) 建立项目级水印比较框架，基于模块级相似度的对称聚合；(2) 提出加权方案，赋予较大模块更高权重，减少小模块噪声影响；(3) 提出部分相似性方法，聚焦相似度最高的前若干模块对，实现部分复用的鲁棒检测。

Result: 在35个开源Java项目（10个类别）上评估，将同一项目的不同版本视为复用案例。使用水印的韧性（resilience）和可信度（credibility）的调和均值作为评价指标。所提方法一致优于现有方法，实现了项目级别部分代码复用的鲁棒且稳定的检测。

Conclusion: 所提出的项目级水印比较框架及加权+部分相似性机制能有效解决部分复用和小模块偶然相似性问题，为项目级别的代码抄袭检测提供了更实用、更鲁棒的解决方案。

Abstract: Software birthmarks provide a robust approach to detecting code plagiarism even under substantial modifications, while distinguishing independently developed software. Existing similarity measures are typically applied at the module level (e.g., source or class files). However, in practice, software reuse often occurs at the project level, where only a subset of modules may be reused. This setting introduces two key challenges: (1) partial reuse, where reused modules constitute only a small fraction of the project, and (2) incidental similarity from small modules, which can lead to false positives.
  In this paper, we establish a framework for project-wise birthmark comparison based on a symmetric aggregation of module-level similarities. On top of this framework, we propose two complementary mechanisms to address the above challenges. First, we introduce a weighting scheme that assigns higher importance to larger modules, reducing the influence of noisy matches from small modules. Second, we propose a partial similarity method that focuses on the top fraction of highly similar module pairs, enabling robust detection of partial reuse.
  We evaluate the proposed approach on 35 open-source Java projects across ten categories, where different versions of the same project are treated as reuse cases. The dataset and experimental artifacts are made publicly available to support reproducibility. Performance is assessed using two complementary properties of software birthmarks, resilience and credibility, combined via their harmonic mean. The results show that the proposed method consistently outperforms existing approaches, achieving robust and stable detection of partial code reuse at the project level.

</details>


### [195] [Unlocking Model Potentials Through Adaptive Multi-Agent Scaffolding for Efficient Issue Resolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25514)
*Yang Chen,Aliya Ahmad,Yiheng Zhou,Reyhaneh Jabbarvand*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: icat-agent是一种去中心化多智能体框架，通过同步事件驱动消息传递替代共享上下文，并利用基于量规的问题质量检查来动态调整工作流程。在SWE-bench Verified和SWE-bench Pro上，icat-agent显著优于多个基线方法，性能提升3.6-18.5%，同时降低了计算成本。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理方法在处理复杂bug时面临上下文管理低效、上下文退化与中毒问题，导致无法成功解决需要长跨度工作流的复杂软件工程问题。

Method: 提出icat-agent框架：1) 去中心化多智能体架构，用同步事件驱动消息传递替代共享上下文；2) 基于量规的问题质量检查机制，对高质量问题并行打补丁与验证，对低质量问题先进行探索。

Abstract: Resolving issues with ambiguous and incomplete descriptions, particularly concerning complex bugs, requires a sophisticated, long-horizon workflow. Agents must navigate codebases to locate the root cause, reproduce the failure, implement a fix, and validate the resulting patch. Inefficient context management, thereby, can lead to rapid context degradation and context poisoning, preventing successful resolution. We propose icat-agent, a decentralized, multi-agent scaffolding that replaces shared context with synchronous, event-based message passing. Utilizing a rubric-based issue quality check, icat-agent strategically pivots its workflow: it initiates parallel patching and validation for well-defined issues, while deploying preliminary exploration for low-quality ones. A comprehensive evaluation of icat-agent on SWE-bench Verified and SWE-bench Pro demonstrates that it consistently outperforms prominent baselines across all difficulty levels, including SWE-agent, mini-SWE-agent, and Claude Code, while using the same underlying models, improving by 3.6-8.4% on SWE-bench Verified and 6.3-18.5% on SWE-bench Pro. icat-agent is also computationally efficient, reducing the average cost by $1.18 per instance compared with the multi-agent Claude Code baseline. Our findings reveal that a robust scaffold such as icat-agent unlocks substantial latent capability within a fixed model, with the same backbone resolving markedly more issues under icat-agent than under existing scaffolds. icat-agent +GPT-5.4-xhigh resolves 67.4% of SWE-bench Pro problems, outperforming the current best result on SWE-bench Pro (59.10%, mini-SWE-agent+GPT-5.4-xhigh) by 8.3 percentage points.

### [197] [Evaluating LLMs on Real-World Software Performance Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25530)
*Ezgi Sarıkayak,Wenchao Gu,Hesham Ghonim,Chunyang Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出SWE-Pro基准，用于评估LLM在真实仓库级代码性能优化中的能力，发现当前LLM在运行时优化和内存优化上均远不及人类专家。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准过度简化了性能优化问题，忽视执行时间与内存的权衡、测量噪声、输入变化等因素，缺乏真实仓库级评估。

Method: 从开源项目中收集102个专家编写的优化任务，构建SWE-Pro基准，使用参数化测试在噪声感知条件下评估运行时、峰值内存和TWMU。

Abstract: Software performance optimization is a notoriously complex and manual task. Despite the growing use of Large Language Models (LLMs) for code refinement, we still lack benchmarks that capture how optimization actually happens in real-world codebases. Existing frameworks often oversimplify the problem by focusing on isolated functions or a single performance metric, missing the critical trade-offs between execution time and memory footprint, the inherent noise of the measurement environment, and the variability introduced by different input data and execution conditions. We address this by introducing SWE-Pro, a repository-level benchmark derived from 102 expert-written optimizations from open-source projects. Unlike previous benchmarks, SWE-Pro pairs each task with parameterized tests to evaluate runtime, peak memory, and Time-Weighted Memory Usage (TWMU) across varying input data and execution conditions under noise-aware measurement conditions. Our evaluation shows that current LLMs struggle significantly: runtime gains are negligible, and memory optimizations are nearly non-existent. This stands in sharp contrast to expert implementations, which achieve an aggregate speedup of 15.5x and peak memory reduction of 171.3x over benchmark tasks. Expert-written improvements are observed in 91.2% of tasks for runtime and 65.7% for peak memory. Our findings expose a substantial gap between current LLM capabilities and the demands of expert-level engineering.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需求工程实证研究缺乏同时包含源代码和对应需求的数据集，研究者试图利用LLM从现有代码库合成需求以填补这一空白。

Method: 采用基于LLM和RAG支持的智能体方法，从源代码生成需求，通过人在回路验证实现状态，并合成引入需求异味和未实现需求。

Result: LLM无法可靠生成非实现需求（i）、无法生成高质量需求（ii）、无法可靠引入合成需求异味（iii）；单一LLM或单一人无法可靠检测需求异味。

Abstract: Empirical research in Requirements Engineering is hampered by a lack of adequate datasets that pair source code with corresponding requirements. A tempting route to addressing this lack is the use of Large Language Models to synthesize requirements from existing code bases. We investigate this question by evaluating an LLM-based and RAG-supported agentic approach that generates requirements from source code, verifies their implementation status relying on a human-in-the-loop, and synthetically introduces requirements smells and non-implemented requirements. Our goal was to create datasets that mimic reality and foster empirical RE research. However, during the study, various problems arose, leading to this experience report. Contrary to our initial hypotheses, LLMs were unable to (i) generate non-implemented requirements reliably, (ii) generate high quality requirements, and (iii) reliably introduce synthetic requirements smells. Furthermore, neither an LLM nor a single human-in-the-loop suffices to detect requirements smells reliably. These findings suggest that the generation of code-to-requirements datasets using LLMs is not yet viable and requires human supervision, especially for quality assurance. We critically reflect on our lessons learned and draw relevant conclusions for both researchers and practitioners.

### [199] [IntentTester: Intent-Driven Multi-agent Framework for Cross-Library Test Migration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25588)
*Yi Gao,Ziyuan Zhang,Xing Hu,Xiaohu Yang,Xin Xia*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: IntentTester是一个基于多智能体框架的意图驱动测试复用系统，通过将测试抽象为语言无关的测试描述语言（TDL），结合知识图谱对齐语义实体，实现跨库、跨语言的测试迁移。在9个开源项目上生成2,776个语法正确测试（85%正确率），74%执行成功，并发现了被维护者确认的缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单元测试中蕴含的领域知识被锁定在单个项目内，难以跨库复用。现有基于结构代码映射（如API签名）的迁移方法在跨语言或设计差异大的场景下失效，生成的迁移测试不可执行。

Method: 提出IntentTester多智能体框架：(1) 将测试抽象为语言无关的测试描述语言（TDL）；(2) 利用知识图谱对齐语义相关的实体和依赖；(3) 通过LLM引导推理和迭代验证合成可执行测试，无需人工干预。

Result: 在JSON、HTML、Time三个领域、Java和Python两种语言的9个开源项目上评估：生成2,776个语法正确测试（85%正确率，基线分别为51%和43%），2,410个执行成功（74%有效率），发现栈溢出、空指针、解析不一致等缺陷并获维护者确认/修复。

Conclusion: 意图驱动的测试迁移从代码映射转向语义对齐，使得跨库、跨语言测试复用变得可行，同时提升了测试质量并暴露了实现缺陷。

Abstract: Unit tests capture both functional checks and domain-specific knowledge, but this knowledge remains locked within individual projects and is rarely reused across libraries with overlapping functionality. Existing migration techniques based on structural code mappings (e.g., API signatures) often break down under divergent designs or cross-language settings, resulting in non-executable migrated tests. In this paper, we present IntentTester, a multi-agent framework for intent-driven test reuse. Instead of translating raw code, IntentTester abstracts tests into a language-agnostic Test Description Language (TDL), aligns them with semantically related entities and dependencies in a repository graph, and synthesizes executable tests through LLM-guided reasoning and iterative validation. This design enables cross-library and cross-language migration without manual intervention, producing migrated tests that existing structure-mapping approaches cannot achieve. We evaluate IntentTester on nine open-source projects across three domains (JSON, HTML, and Time) and two languages (Java and Python). IntentTester generates 2,776 syntactically correct tests with 85\% correctness; in comparison, the two baselines achieve 51\% and 43\%. Among them, 2,410 tests executed successfully, yielding a 74\% effectiveness rate. Beyond higher success rates, IntentTester also surfaced previously unknown defects including stack overflows, null dereferences, and parsing inconsistencies, several of which have been acknowledged or patched by maintainers. Our results show that intent-driven migration shifts the focus from code mappings to semantic alignment, allowing practical cross-library and cross-language test reuse while improving test quality and exposing implementation flaws.

### [200] [CodeChat-Eval: Evaluating Large Language Models in Multi-Turn Code Refinement Dialogues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25747)
*Guoxiang,Guo,Kla Tantithamthavorn,Neelofar Neelofar,Yuanyuan Qi,Aldeida Aleti*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used in software engineering to generate and refine code. In practice, developers often continue from an initial code generation request with follow-up refinement instructions, such as requests to improve style, restructure implementation, or change the execution strategy while preserving the intended behaviour. However, existing benchmarks generally omit this multi-turn code refinement dialogue setting and therefore cannot evaluate whether LLMs maintain functional correctness, i.e., whether the refined code still passes the test suite for the original task. To address this limitation, we introduce CodeChat-Eval, an evaluation framework that constructs evaluation sessions from multi-turn code refinement dialogues using a dynamic instruction selection algorithm. Our empirical study on open-weight and proprietary LLMs observes a statistically significant decrease ranging from 19.2% (GPT-5 Nano) to 69.2% (Llama 3.1 8B) in functional correctness over multi-turn refinement. The largest correctness drops are associated with logic-level refinements and additive change requests. These findings indicate that LLMs struggle to maintain functional correctness during multi-turn code refinement dialogues, and highlight the need for benchmarks that evaluate functionality-preserving refinement beyond single-turn generation.

### [201] [Automated Detection of Configuration-Specific Security Vulnerabilities via Patch Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25863)
*Felipe de Sant'Anna Paixão,Joanna C. S. Santos,Paulo Anselmo da Mota Silveira Neto,Daniel Sadoc Menasche,Gustavo Bittencourt Figueiredo,Eduardo Santana de Almeida*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出PatchLens，一种纯静态技术，通过分析补丁和配置条件来恢复漏洞影响条件(VIC)，无需编译即可精确描述哪些编译变体包含漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高度可配置的C/C++系统中，安全补丁只修复特定配置变体下的漏洞，但现有方法难以精确定位漏洞影响哪些编译变体，且CVE描述几乎不包含配置信息，导致漏洞评估和修复验证不完整。

Method: 形式化定义漏洞影响条件(VIC)为配置选项上的布尔谓词；提出PatchLens纯静态技术，通过对齐AST级补丁块与源码级存在条件，并结合轻量级构建系统分析解析文件包含关系，恢复VIC。

Result: 在Linux内核(1192个补丁)、FFmpeg(289个)和PHP(100个)上评估，VIC紧凑(平均变量数分别为1.84、3.23、1.04)，仅有少数漏洞是系统范围的（这类漏洞CVSS分数更高）；CVE文本几乎不编码必要选项(召回率约1%)。

Conclusion: PatchLens可扩展、可解释，能应用于CI中的变体感知分诊与测试选择、定向采样与模糊测试、特征风险评分等场景，为高度可配置软件的漏洞评估提供实用路径。

Abstract: We study how security patches in highly configurable C/C++ systems map onto the space of compile-time variants. We formalize the Vulnerability Impact Condition (VIC) - a Boolean predicate over configuration options that denotes all variants that contained the original flaw - and introduce PatchLens, a purely static technique that recovers VICs by aligning AST-level patch hunks with source-level presence conditions and resolving file inclusion via lightweight build system analysis. Evaluating PatchLens on 1,192 Linux kernel, 289 FFmpeg, and 100 PHP patches, we compute precise, human-readable VICs without the need to compile any system variant. The resulting predicates are compact (avg. 1.84 variables for Linux, 3.23 for FFmpeg, 1.04 for PHP) and show that only a small fraction of vulnerabilities are system-wide, which carry higher CVSS scores; meanwhile, CVE texts almost never encode the required options ($\approx$ 1% average recall), motivating automated enrichment of CVE descriptions with VICs. PatchLens and the accompanying dataset enable immediate applications in CI (variant-aware triage and test selection), targeted sampling and fuzzing, and feature risk scoring, offering a scalable, explainable path to vulnerability assessment in highly configurable software.

### [202] [LLM-Based Discovery of Latent Requirements from Stakeholder Conversations: Preliminary Results from Industry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25867)
*Mithila Sivakumar,Martin Lochner,Shiva Nejati,Mehrdad Sabetzadeh*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: LENS是一种利用LLM分析利益相关者访谈记录的方法，不仅能提取显式需求，还能推断隐含需求，并通过用户故事和原文追溯确保可追溯性。在工业网络安全场景中，显式需求提取F1达84.4%，75%的隐含需求被领域专家认为具有实用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利益相关者访谈是需求获取的重要来源，但许多相关需求在对话中往往是隐式的，未被明确表述。现有方法主要关注显式需求的提取，忽略了隐含需求的挖掘机会。

Method: LENS方法利用LLM分析访谈记录，一方面提取显式需求，另一方面结合组织工具和基础设施的上下文信息，推理并推断隐含需求。所有需求均以用户故事形式呈现，并与访谈原文片段链接以确保可追溯性。

Result: 在12份工业网络安全领域的利益相关者访谈记录上评估，显式需求提取平均F1得分为84.4%；对于LENS识别的隐含需求，平均有75%被领域专家认为具有自动化或节省时间的潜力。

Conclusion: LENS能够有效从访谈中提取显式需求并推断有价值的隐含需求，为需求获取提供更全面的自动化支持。

Abstract: Stakeholder interviews are an important source of information for requirements elicitation, yet many relevant requirements remain implicit in such conversations. Stakeholders frequently describe workflows, challenges, and operational practices without explicitly articulating the software capabilities that could address them. Recent work has considered the use of LLMs to analyze conversational data and extract requirements from stakeholder interviews. Existing approaches, however, primarily focus on identifying explicitly stated requirements, leaving implicit opportunities largely unexplored. In this paper, we present LENS (LLM-Enabled Needs Discovery from Stakeholder Interviews), an approach that analyzes stakeholder interview transcripts to both extract explicit requirements and infer additional latent requirements. LENS performs this inference by reasoning over stakeholder statements together with contextual information about organizational tools and infrastructure. Both extracted and inferred requirements are represented as user stories and linked to transcript excerpts to ensure traceability. We conduct a preliminary evaluation of LENS using twelve stakeholder interview transcripts collected in an industrial setting involving cybersecurity operations. We show that LENS achieves an average F1-score of 84.4% for extracting explicit requirements, while, on average, 75% of the latent requirements identified by LENS were perceived as providing useful automation or time-saving potential by domain experts.

</details>


### [203] [The Web4 Agent Economy: A Large-Scale Empirical Study of the Landscape, Challenges, and Opportunities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25876)
*Yuhan Jin,Shuohan Wu,Chong Chen,Lingfeng Bao,Xiaohu Yang,Jiachi Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文首次大规模实证研究Web4代理生态系统，分析了99,448个多链身份注册、3.17亿+交易日志、341个MCP项目源码和349个GitHub问题。研究发现自主代理已建立活跃的机器对机器支付经济（日均数百万交易），但基础设施仍不成熟，存在身份/授权、跨环境操作和支付互操作性等挑战，社区响应分布不均，支付互操作性是最大瓶颈。

  <summary>Details</summary>
